		focus = FAT_chaos_in_the_countryside
	}
	mutually_exclusive = {
		focus = FAT_plactate_the_generals
	}
	x = -4
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = FAT_chaos_in_the_countryside
	cost = 2
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 70
	}
	available = {
		has_country_flag = reform_military
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus FAT_reform_the_military"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = griffonRepublic.10
				days = 60
			}
		}
		add_war_support = 0.04
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = -0.04
		}
		add_political_power = -40
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL FOCUS_FILTER_WAR_SUPPORT }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = FAT_sack_the_commanders
	icon = GFX_goal_purge_opposition
	prerequisite = {
		focus = FAT_presidents_speech
	}
	x = -2
	y = 3
	relative_position_id = FAT_reform_the_military
	cost = 4
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 50
	}
	bypass = {
		OR = {
			has_civil_war = yes
			country_exists = FAW
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus FAT_sack_the_commanders"
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = 0.025
		custom_effect_tooltip = FAT_sack_the_commanders_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			FAT_claus_rosewing = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_unit_leader = yes
					}
					remove_unit_leader_role = yes
					remove_advisor_role = { slot = political_advisor }
				}
			}
			FAT_reinhard_suntail = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_unit_leader = yes
					}
					remove_unit_leader_role = yes
					remove_advisor_role = { slot = political_advisor }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_STABILITY FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = FAT_loyality_to_the_republic
	icon = GFX_goal_revolution
	prerequisite = {
		focus = FAT_a_new_army
	}
	mutually_exclusive = {
		focus = FAT_loyality_to_the_president
	}
	continue_if_invalid = no
	cancel_if_invalid = yes
	available = {
		has_civil_war = no
		hidden_trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = FAW
			}
		}
	}
	x = -1
	y = 5
	relative_position_id = FAT_reform_the_military
	cost = 3
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 50
	}

					has_idea = FAT_Chaos_idea

				limit = {
					has_idea = FAT_Chaos_idea1
				}

					id = griffonRepublic.21
					days = 7
					random = 480					#days to hours applied
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = griffonRepublic.22
					days = 7
					random = 480					#days to hours applied
				}
			}
		}
	}

		}

			hidden_effect = {

					id = griffonRepublic.44

					random = 720					#days to hours applied
				}
			}
		}
	}

				target = BRZ

		}

			}

					type = annex_everything 
					target = YAL
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = { 
				type = annex_everything 
				target = YAL
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_rule = {
				can_only_justify_war_on_threat_country = no
			}
		}
		add_state_claim = 382
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
				OR = {
					is_core_of = GRI
					is_core_of = FEA

					is_core_of = PYT
					is_core_of = ROU
					is_core_of = YAL
					is_core_of = ANG

		}
	}

		every_other_country = {
			limit = {

					NOT = {
						is_feudal_vassal = yes
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = GRD
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = common_cause
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = common_cause
			}
		}
	}
